<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">из-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">iz-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дать.html>дать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">datʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:издеваться.html>издева́ться</a> (5767)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">из-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">iz-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:девать.html>дева́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">devátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:издеваться.html>издева́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">izdevátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поиздеваться.html>поиздева́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to jeer, to scoff, to bully, to taunt
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2009</b>,  Мариам Петросян (<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Mariam_Petrosyan" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Mariam Petrosyan">Mariam Petrosyan</a>),  “Некоторые <a href = vnd.unilang:преимущество.html>преиму́щества</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:спортивный.html>спорти́вной</a> обуви”, in  <cite><a href = vnd.unilang:дом.html>Дом</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:который.html>кото́ром</a>...</cite>, volume 1 |  translated as  “Certain Advantages to Athletic Footwear”, in Marian Schwartz, transl., <cite>The Gray House</cite>, 2017:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́тим</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>как</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:бы.html>бы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:подчеркивать.html>подчёркивает</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:наш.html>на́шу</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:общий.html>о́бщую</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:беда.html>беду́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:считаться.html>счита́ясь</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>на́ми</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:наш.html>на́шим</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мнение.html>мне́нием</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>В</a> како́м-то <a href = vnd.unilang:смысл.html>смы́сле</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> по-сво́ему <b><a href = vnd.unilang:издеваться.html>издева́ется</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:над.html>над</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>на́ми</a>...</span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Étim on kak by podčórkivajet nášu óbščuju bedú ne sčitájasʹ s námi i nášim mnénijem. V kakóm-to smýsle on po-svójemu <b>izdevájetsja</b> nad námi...</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">By doing that it's like he's emphasizing our common misfortune without taking us or our opinion into account. In a sense, he's <b>making fun</b> of us in his own way.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>

***издержка.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:издержка.html>изде́ржка</a> (11457)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">издержа́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">izderžátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:смекалка.html>-к</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-k</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; since the 16th century.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:издержка.html>изде́ржка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">izdéržka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:издержка.html>изде́ржки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:издержка.html>изде́ржки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:издержка.html>изде́ржек</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li class="senseid" id="Russian-expense"><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">usually plural</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> expenses, costs</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:изжога.html>изжо́га</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">izžóga</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:изжога.html>изжо́ги</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:изжога.html>изжо́ги</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:изжога.html>изжо́г</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>heartburn, pyrosis
<ul><li><div class="wiktQuote" data-validation="white">Александр Солженицын, <i>Матренин <a href = vnd.unilang:двор.html>двор</a></i> 1968:<dl><dd><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:после.html>по́сле</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:еда.html>еды́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:оставлять.html>оставля́ло</a> налёт <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> нёбе, <a href = vnd.unilang:десна.html>дёснах</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вызывать.html>вызыва́ло</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:изжога.html>изжо́гу</a></b></span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">pósle jedý ostavljálo naljót na njóbe, djósnax i vyzyválo <b>izžógu</b></i></dd><dd>after eating a smack lingered both palate and gums and caused <b>heartburn</b></dd></dl></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:из.html>из</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>жо́<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:га.html>га</a></b>
